<p>The <i><a href="/wiki/J%C5%8Dy%C5%8D_kanji" title="Jōyō kanji">jōyō kanji</a></i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja"><span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">常用漢字</span></span></span></span>, <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1177148991">.mw-parser-output .IPA-label-small{font-size:85%}.mw-parser-output .references .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .infobox .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .navbox .IPA-label-small{font-size:100%}</style><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">Japanese pronunciation:</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="ja-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Japanese" title="Help:IPA/Japanese">&#91;dʑoːjoːkaꜜɲdʑi&#93;</a></span>, lit. "regular-use kanji")</span> system of representing written <a href="/wiki/Japanese_language" title="Japanese language">Japanese</a> currently consists of 2,136 characters.
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="List_of_characters">List of characters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_j%C5%8Dy%C5%8D_kanji&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: List of characters"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>For brevity, only one English translation is given per <a href="/wiki/Kanji" title="Kanji">kanji</a>.</li>
<li>The "Grade" column specifies the grade in which the kanji is taught in <a href="/wiki/Elementary_schools_in_Japan" title="Elementary schools in Japan">Elementary schools in Japan</a>. Grade "S" means that it is taught in <a href="/wiki/Secondary_school" title="Secondary school">secondary school</a>.</li>
<li>The list is sorted by Japanese reading (<a href="/wiki/Kanji#On&#39;yomi_(Sino-Japanese_reading)" title="Kanji">on'yomi</a> in <a href="/wiki/Katakana" title="Katakana">katakana</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Kanji#Kun&#39;yomi_(native_reading)" title="Kanji">kun'yomi</a> in <a href="/wiki/Hiragana" title="Hiragana">hiragana</a>), in accordance with the ordering in the official Jōyō table.</li>
<li>This list does not include characters that were present in older versions of the list but have since been removed (<span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja"><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E5%8B%BA" class="extiw" title="wikt:勺">勺</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E9%8A%91" class="extiw" title="wikt:銑">銑</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E8%84%B9" class="extiw" title="wikt:脹">脹</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E9%8C%98" class="extiw" title="wikt:錘">錘</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%E5%8C%81" class="extiw" title="wikt:匁">匁</a></span></span>).</li>
<li>Hyphens in the kun'yomi readings separate kanji from their <a href="/wiki/Okurigana" title="Okurigana">okurigana</a>.</li>
<li>The "New" column attempts to reflect the official glyph shapes as closely as possible. This requires using the characters 𠮟, 塡, 剝, 頰 which are outside of Japan's basic character set, <a href="/wiki/JIS_X_0208" title="JIS X 0208">JIS X 0208</a> (one of them is also outside the Unicode BMP). In practice, these characters are usually replaced by the characters 叱, 填, 剥, 頬, which are present in JIS X 0208.</li>
<li>The "Old" column reflects the official <a href="/wiki/Ky%C5%ABjitai" title="Kyūjitai">kyūjitai</a> specified in the standard jōyō table;<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> it does not include unofficial, extended, or <a href="/wiki/Asahi_characters" title="Asahi characters">Asahi characters</a>.<sup class="noprint selfreference">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Talk:List_of_j%C5%8Dy%C5%8D_kanji#Kanji_variants" title="Talk:List of jōyō kanji">discuss</a></i>&#93;</sup></li>
<li>The readings presented here are those noted in the official Jōyō table.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> Special readings and uncommon readings are indicated in brackets.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> Other readings (generally less common, such as the <a href="/wiki/Nanori" title="Nanori">nanori</a>) may also exist.</li></ul>
<table lang="ja" class="sortable wikitable" style="font-family: &#39;Calibri&#39;, &#39;Ubuntu&#39;, &#39;ヒラギノ角ゴシック W3&#39;,&#39;ヒラギノ角ゴシック&#39;,&#39;Hiragino Sans&#39;,&#39;メイリオ&#39;,Meiryo,&#39;新ゴ Pr6N R&#39;,&#39;A-OTF 新ゴ Pr6N R&#39;,&#39;小塚ゴシック Pr6N M&#39;,&#39;IPAexゴシック&#39;,&#39;Takaoゴシック&#39;,&#39;XANO明朝U32&#39;,&#39;XANO明朝&#39;,&#39;和田研中丸ゴシック2004絵文字&#39;,&#39;和田研中丸ゴシック2004ARIB&#39;,&#39;和田研中丸ゴシック2004P4&#39;,&#39;和田研細丸ゴシック2004絵文字&#39;,&#39;和田研細丸ゴシック2004ARIB&#39;,&#39;和田研細丸ゴシック2004P4&#39;,&#39;和田研細丸ゴシックProN&#39;,&#39;IPA Pゴシック&#39;,&#39;ＭＳ Ｐゴシック&#39;;">

cite.citation{font-style:inherit;word-wrap:break-word}.mw-parser-output .citation q{quotes:"\"""\"""'""'"}.mw-parser-output .citation:target{background-color:rgba(0,127,255,0.133)}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-free.id-lock-free a{background:url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/6/65/Lock-green.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}body:not(.skin-timeless):not(.skin-minerva) .mw-parser-output .id-lock-free a{background-size:contain}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-limited.id-lock-limited a,.mw-parser-output .id-lock-registration.id-lock-registration a,body:not(.skin-timeless):not(.skin-minerva) .mw-parser-output .id-lock-registration a{background-size:contain}.mw-parser-output .id-lock-subscription.id-lock-subscription a{background:url("//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/aa/Lock-red-alt-2.svg")right 0.1em center/9px no-repeat}body:not(.skin-timeless):not(.skin-minerva) .mw-parser-output .id-lock-subscription .cs1-code{color:inherit;background:inherit;border:none;padding:inherit}.mw-parser-output .cs1-hidden-error{display:none;color:#d33}.mw-parser-output .cs1-visible-error{color:#d33}.mw-parser-output .cs1-maint{display:none;color:#2C882D;margin-left:0.3em}.mw-parser-output .cs1-format{font-size:95%}.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-left{padding-left:0.2em}.mw-parser-output .cs1-kern-right{padding-right:0.2em}.mw-parser-output .citation .mw-selflink{font-weight:inherit}html.skin-theme-clientpref-night .mw-parser-output .cs1-maint{color:#18911F}html.skin-theme-clientpref-night .mw-parser-output .cs1-visible-error,html.skin-theme-clientpref-night .mw-parser-output .cs1-hidden-error{color:#f8a397}@media(prefers-color-scheme:dark){html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .cs1-visible-error,html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .cs1-hidden-error{color:#f8a397}html.skin-theme-clientpref-os .mw-parser-output .cs1-maint{color:#18911F}}</style><cite class="citation web cs1 cs1-prop-script cs1-prop-foreign-lang-source"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bunka.go.jp/kokugo_nihongo/sisaku/joho/joho/kijun/naikaku/pdf/joyokanjihyo_20101130.pdf">"Jōyō Kanji Hyō" <bdi lang="ja">常用漢字表</bdi></a> &#91;List of Joyo Kanji&#93; <span class="cs1-format">(PDF)</span> (in Japanese). Agency of Cultural Affairs, Government of Japan<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">November 7,</span> 2018</span>.</cite><span title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=J%C5%8Dy%C5%8D+Kanji+Hy%C5%8D+%E5%B8%B8%E7%94%A8%E6%BC%A2%E5%AD%97%E8%A1%A8&amp;rft.pub=Agency+of+Cultural+Affairs%2C+Government+of+Japan&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.bunka.go.jp%2Fkokugo_nihongo%2Fsisaku%2Fjoho%2Fjoho%2Fkijun%2Fnaikaku%2Fpdf%2Fjoyokanjihyo_20101130.pdf&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AList+of+j%C5%8Dy%C5%8D+kanji" class="Z3988"></span></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-3"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-3">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">See <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.bunka.go.jp/kokugo_nihongo/sisaku/joho/joho/kijun/naikaku/pdf/joyokanjihyo_20101130.pdf">[1]</a>, page 2, bullet point 7: "Readings indented one character to the right are special readings, or readings with very narrow use. Indented reading for which a prefecture name is indicated in the 'Remarks' column are, as a general rule, only ever used in the specified prefecture name."</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-B-4"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-5"><sup><i><b>f</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-6"><sup><i><b>g</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-7"><sup><i><b>h</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-8"><sup><i><b>i</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-9"><sup><i><b>j</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-10"><sup><i><b>k</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-11"><sup><i><b>l</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-12"><sup><i><b>m</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-13"><sup><i><b>n</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-14"><sup><i><b>o</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-15"><sup><i><b>p</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-16"><sup><i><b>q</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-17"><sup><i><b>r</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-18"><sup><i><b>s</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-19"><sup><i><b>t</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-20"><sup><i><b>u</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-21"><sup><i><b>v</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-22"><sup><i><b>w</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-23"><sup><i><b>x</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-24"><sup><i><b>y</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-25"><sup><i><b>z</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-26"><sup><i><b>aa</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-27"><sup><i><b>ab</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-28"><sup><i><b>ac</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-29"><sup><i><b>ad</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-30"><sup><i><b>ae</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-31"><sup><i><b>af</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-32"><sup><i><b>ag</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-33"><sup><i><b>ah</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-34"><sup><i><b>ai</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-35"><sup><i><b>aj</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-36"><sup><i><b>ak</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-37"><sup><i><b>al</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-38"><sup><i><b>am</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-39"><sup><i><b>an</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-40"><sup><i><b>ao</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-41"><sup><i><b>ap</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-42"><sup><i><b>aq</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-43"><sup><i><b>ar</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-44"><sup><i><b>as</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-45"><sup><i><b>at</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-46"><sup><i><b>au</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-47"><sup><i><b>av</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-48"><sup><i><b>aw</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-49"><sup><i><b>ax</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-50"><sup><i><b>ay</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-51"><sup><i><b>az</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-52"><sup><i><b>ba</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-53"><sup><i><b>bb</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-54"><sup><i><b>bc</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-55"><sup><i><b>bd</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-56"><sup><i><b>be</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-57"><sup><i><b>bf</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-58"><sup><i><b>bg</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-59"><sup><i><b>bh</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-60"><sup><i><b>bi</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-B_4-61"><sup><i><b>bj</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">These characters are <a href="/wiki/Unicode" title="Unicode">Unicode</a> <a href="/wiki/CJK_Unified_Ideographs" title="CJK Unified Ideographs">CJK Unified Ideographs</a> for which the old form (kyūjitai) and the new form (shinjitai) have been unified under the Unicode standard. Although the old and new forms are distinguished under the JIS X 0213 standard, the old forms map to Unicode <a href="/wiki/CJK_Unified_Ideographs#CJK_Compatibility_Ideographs" title="CJK Unified Ideographs">CJK Compatibility Ideographs</a> which are considered by Unicode to be <a href="/wiki/Unicode_equivalence" title="Unicode equivalence">canonically equivalent</a> to the new forms and may not be distinguished by user agents. Therefore depending on the user environment, it may not be possible to see the distinction between old and new forms of the characters. In particular, all <a href="/wiki/Unicode_equivalence" title="Unicode equivalence">Unicode normalization</a> methods merge the old characters with the new ones.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-C-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-C_5-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-C_5-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-C_5-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-C_5-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-C_5-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The 5 kanji <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">茨・牙・韓・&#134047;・栃</span></span> have <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bunka.go.jp/kokugo_nihongo/sisaku/joho/joho/kijun/naikaku/pdf/joyokanjihyo_20101130.pdf#page=6">specifically designated design variations</a> described in the official Jōyō Kanji list, which apply only to those individual kanji.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-D-6"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-D_6-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-D_6-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-D_6-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-D_6-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-D_6-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">These kanji readings are offset by one character to the right in the official Jōyō Kanji list, and are followed by a Japanese prefecture name in the remarks column. Therefore, in principle, these readings will only ever be used for those specific prefecture names and not in any other words.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-E-7"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-5"><sup><i><b>f</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-6"><sup><i><b>g</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-7"><sup><i><b>h</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-8"><sup><i><b>i</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-9"><sup><i><b>j</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-10"><sup><i><b>k</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-11"><sup><i><b>l</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-12"><sup><i><b>m</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-E_7-13"><sup><i><b>n</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The official Jōyō Kanji list states that "Due to the print typefaces which are currently available in computer systems, it is acceptable to use characters different from the ones show in this list (e.g. using <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">頬・</span></span>賭<span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">・剥</span></span> instead of <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">頰・賭・剝</span></span>, etc.)". Although the official document does not specifically designate the characters which this statement applies to, it is likely that it is applicable to the following 14 characters: <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">淫・葛・僅・煎・詮・嘲・捗・溺・塡・賭・剝・箸・蔽・頰</span></span>.</span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-G-8"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-G_8-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-G_8-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-G_8-2"><sup><i><b>c</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-G_8-3"><sup><i><b>d</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-G_8-4"><sup><i><b>e</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">The 5 kanji <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">餌・遡・遜・謎・餅</span></span> use one of the radicals <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">辶</span></span> / <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">&#169599;</span></span>. As stated on the first page of the official Jōyō Kanji list, although the officially correct form of those characters uses the forms <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">辶</span></span> / <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">&#169599;</span></span>, it is permissible to use instead the forms <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">&#64102;</span></span> / <span title="Japanese-language text"><span lang="ja">飠</span></span>, which are indicated in square brackets in the official list.</span>
</li>
</ol></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="External_links">External links</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_j%C5%8Dy%C5%8D_kanji&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: External links"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1217611005">.mw-parser-output .side-box{margin:4px 0;box-sizing:border-box;border:1px solid #aaa;font-size:88%;line-height:1.25em;background-color:#f9f9f9;display:flow-root}.mw-parser-output .side-box-abovebelow,.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{padding:0.25em 0.9em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-image{padding:2px 0 2px 0.9em;text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-imageright{padding:2px 0.9em 2px 0;text-align:center}@media(min-width:500px){.mw-parser-output .side-box-flex{display:flex;align-items:center}.mw-parser-output .side-box-text{flex:1;min-width:0}}@media(min-width:720px){.mw-parser-output .side-box{width:238px}.mw-parser-output .side-box-right{clear:right;float:right;margin-left:1em}.mw-parser-output .side-box-left{margin-right:1em}}</style><div class="side-box side-box-right plainlinks sistersitebox"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1126788409">
<div class="side-box-flex">
<div class="side-box-image"><span class="noviewer" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Wiktionary-logo-en-v2.svg/40px-Wiktionary-logo-en-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Wiktionary-logo-en-v2.svg/60px-Wiktionary-logo-en-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/99/Wiktionary-logo-en-v2.svg/80px-Wiktionary-logo-en-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="512" /></span></span></div>
<div class="side-box-text plainlist">Look up <i><b><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Appendix:Joyo_kanji_by_reading" class="extiw" title="wiktionary:Appendix:Joyo kanji by reading">Appendix:Joyo kanji by reading</a></b></i>&#160;or <i><b><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/List_of_j%C5%8Dy%C5%8D_kanji" class="extiw" title="wiktionary:List of jōyō kanji">List of jōyō kanji</a></b></i> in Wiktionary, the free dictionary.</div></div>
